I cannot suggest strongly enough that you NOT go here. I 100% agree with the other reviewers who say that they had issues with their crowns, rude staff, and that it's very expensive and the services are more money than care motivated. The only pleasant experience I had here was the removal of my wisdom teeth with an oral surgeon who is an outside contractor and doesn't actually work here. As an example, one day I was here for around 9 hours for 2 fillings-one needed a crown and the other an inlay. During that 9 hour appointment, I had 3 different dentists working on me, including one fresh out of dental school as well as the owner of the practice. Fast forward to a few months later, my crown fell out while chewing. When I went back to get it fixed, it actually needed to be redone again due to decay. A few days after the second crown was redone, a dark line appeared all along my gum line around the tooth and you guessed it... it needed to be redone AGAIN. Even now, the crown is bulky and ill-fitting, but there's no way in hell I would let them have a 4th go at it. Stay away!!!</Review>

I was always petrified to go to the dentist. Dr Neil and his assistant at Redlands dental changed that for me! They were very professional yet very careful to make me feel secure that I would be ok! To me this was very important as I was so fearful which also made their job more difficult but they helped me overcome my fears! I read a lot of reviews complaining about price but I did not find them to be overpriced and also realize that it is very exspensive for one to complete dental school as it also is for doctors, veterinarians ect. So one must take that into consideration. I was so happy with the work I had done and also the fact that they can fit me in when I have an emergency. The manager is also very kind and deeply cares about her employees and goes the extra mile to make sure the company has caring, knowledgeable dentists, hygienists and specialists! I was impressed that they are " up to date" on so many new procedures! I love the staff at Redlands Dental and if your a big sissy like me I highly recommend them!< /Text>

<rating>2<//rating>< Review>
I first showed up just for a cleaning. after the cleaning they told me I needed a crown and a filling. This seemed odd to me because I have had very few dental issues in the past. Unfortunately I let them do the procedure. The day I came back in for my crown the temporary cap came off, leaving an exposed nerve end.

When they sat me down in the chair they immediately began work on installing the crown. Little did I realize that this was about to be the excruciating experience of my life. They first sprayed compressed air directly on my nerve end causing me to jump out of the chair cursing obscenities!!! I told the woman that it hurt, but she didn't seem to care and she pressed on applying a steady stream of cold water to the same exposed nerve. I leaped out of the chair and told her I couldn't take it!!! The dentist replied go ahead and sit down, were almost finished. Reluctantly I sat back down in the chair and we finished the operation.

I have had three knee surgeries and none have been as painful as this procedure without Novocain.

1. I was treated like I was cattle
2. very impersonal and un-empathetic service.
3. They are great at pretending to care.
4. They forgot to use the Novocain!!!!<//Review>

< Review>
June 2017 my husband and I rented a 2nd story apartment with Twin Creeks, This was our first home together as we got married the next month. As it stands today I can not tell you how many management teams there have been in the last 2 years. Lets start at the beginning:

Move-In Day: Delayed for 3 days after original move-in date, never found out why. When we were finally able to move in we noticed there was nothing clean about the apartment in fact we found food in the cabinets so we spent the first day of our delayed move in cleaning what should have been a clean apartment. We noticed we were missing a kitchen window screen and a balcony sliding screen and several blinds and reported that right away, 4 months later we got the screens but never got the blinds. Thankfully I had a friend who lived here who found several in her storage unit when she moved in and she gave us some to fill in the missing holes.

November 2017: Our stove quit working and after putting 2 work orders in the problem has still yet to be resolved. The refrigerator has never gotten cold, we buy our groceries by the day which is kind of annoying.

December 2017: The sliding glass door track broke leaving us unable to close the door a week before Christmas they fixed it, kind of. About this time we started noticing cracks at the ceiling of the fireplace and in fact almost every crease of the ceiling throughout the apartment. We counted 5 cracks and reported them. We were told this is California that is natural.

As the problems continued our kitchen still barely worked in 2018, our washing machine failed twice (guess it is a good thing I work somewhere that has repair people who came to help me because no one responded to those work orders either). Our 5 cracks turned in 18+ now some reaching from ceiling to floor others widening and some are moist.

December 2018: Our bedroom ceiling started leaking yellow water even when the heavy rains or any rain were not happening. We called the office again and that took 2 weeks for roofers to come out but we still have the hole where the water fell from in our bedroom. Near that hole we now have a rapidly growing black substance that is about 2 foot long and 7 inches wide. We suspect that it is mold and have reported it but got nothing from management. Remember that problem with the sliding glass door in 2017 well it happened again it took them 3 weeks this time to fix it cause they had to call door repair people, oh and in case you are wondering the solution offered  by management to the cold rainy weather and the fact we couldn't close our door was turn the heater on.

August 1 2019 WE TURNED IN OUR 30 DAY NOTICE TO MOVE. Also our toilet apparently has been broken and is now flooding our bathroom and the one below it. It is now 8/3 and it still isn't fixed!

In my personal opinion the best advice I can give to anyone who comes to look at this place RUN, DO NOT DO IT! Twin Creeks is not worth the 1700$+ they charge for rent!!! (Included are only a fraction of the cracks that exist in our apartment)

August 9th the plumbers are back but the apartment downstairs is still leaking i have now taking 3 days off of work lets see about a 4th because they don't care that we are trying to pack and leave this hell they only care about the tenant who never should have moved into a broken apartment unit!< /Review>

< Text>
My pet peeve with this place is the misnomer 'Community Market". It has nothing to do with the community, other than being a giant retail chain in the middle of North Berkeley. The name is an insult to the original CO-OP market formerly at this place which WAS a true community market built on the co-op principle. This store is a Safeway, no more no less, with average food and customer service. It does have a good bakery, offering more high end pastries than  the regular Safeways. Other than that, I actually prefer the offerings of the larger Safeway a couple of blocks away. I think Safeway bought the Andronicos stores to get rid of competition. How long will they keep this store open having another, remodeled Safeway just two blocks away?< /Text>
